<rate>5</rate>< Text>
Mr. Appliance is the perfect example of the type of service you HOPE to receive when making this type of call. I had someone out to look at our washing maching, assuming we'd be spending upwards of $250 to fix the issue (a loud rattling noise). The gentleman who came out was super friendly, knowledgeable, and took his time researching the issue. Ultimately he explained that, while it was annoying, the vibration causing the sound was not causing any harm to the washer. And while he could order parts to fix it, the cost would be high, and it wasn't necessary if we could deal with the noise (which we can, since the washer is in our garage). He then took the time to share ways we can easily extend the life of our washer, to get several more years out of it before needing to purchase a new unit.

Ultimately, we ended up HAPPILY paying the $75 consultation fee, and I've since recommended Mr. Appliance to a ton of people. The service we received proves this company understands that being honest and trustworthy will result in a lot more business than taking advantage of customers who aren't very knowledgeable in the product they're seeking help with. We had a sunny breezy weekday for this excursion and enjoyed our visit. 2 large pumpkins were $25 total and should have been $32 according to the price list. Looks like the place has seen better days. Everything looks a little run down. Very dusty. The animals did not look very healthy. But there were pumpkins - lots is them - and many happy kids running around. Concession people were grumpy. Parking and port a potties were a long walk from anywhere. Like I said, all the children visiting appeared to be having a great time which is the whole point!</Text>

<time>1622824042974< /time><rate>5</rate><Gmap_id>0x80dc6e35c448f34b:0x88acab4dd60a70d2</Gmap_id>< review>
Great food for anytime of day.
The breakfast is awesome and I personally like the biscuits and gravy with half bacon and half sausage. The French toast and breakfast burritos are good as well, be careful with their hot sauce. The coffee is usually not burnt as well.

The French fries are made perfectly and is only outdone by the onion rings which are the best especially when compared to a restaurant or bar, be sure to ask for ranch with it.

The smoothies are awesome and can compete with Jamba juice so get the mango smoothie.

There are also beers on tap. Plenty of IPAs for me which makes any meal here feel like a restaurant, sculpin and stone stand out for me.

Mask are enforced which makes me happy, so be sure to bring one.

The drive through was made for a compact vehicle so be sure to take the turn slowly when getting your food.

6/4/21<//review>

< Text>
Everyone loves Angelo's. It's a staple of the local area/culture. They have a huge menu with everything from hamburgers and gyros to burritos and breakfast platters. The food is always reasonably priced and I'm always happy with how much I get for my money. That's probably the biggest selling point for me with this place. The only thing I have against Angelo's are their hamburgers. They put a lot of lettuce and tomato on them, and they just seem to be missing some flavor or pizaz overall. Just my preference though, and everything else is excellent. They even added beer to their menu a few years back.< /Text>

<Name>Bryan ‚ÄúBryan Lupercio‚Äù Lupercio</Name>< review>
What's the thing about Angelo's. It's different. It's unique and it's only in oceanside. They sport the red and yellow. Which at first I thought it was an In N out. But the Hispanic version! There menu is creative and diverse. From gyros, to burgers and burritos. Breakfast all day. Unique desert menu. Your eyes are glued to the big sign in the drive through trying to decide what to pick. The price maybe be a little. But the portions sizes. You will get it for lunch and dinner. You will see these locations scattered as if it was a field of flowers. Don't be fooled. They good. I call it one of Oceanside's unique talents. Whether you dine in our hit the drive through. It's good. The staff has your back when you order extra ranch, unlike other places that charge you a nickle, dime, and if they super stingy. A quarter. Have your wallet full and a deep appetite. Try this place out!</review>

This place is so shockingly dirty and run down it amazes me they are not closed by the health department. They have not repaired so many broken tiles and other surfaces, exposing difficult to clean/porous surfaces, that I am sure roaches must run rampant at night. I normally don't wright reviews but this place was so bad I feel it is my patriotic duty to warn people of it so, here it goes.
I ordered the bacon monster combo and my wife ordered the chicken burger. the hamburger was large but the patty was about 1/4 inch thick. After removing the lettuce I was left with a pretty unimpressive burger, fires and a coke for $10.00. The chicken burger was very thin as well and dry and tasted like leather. It's been sitting in my stomach like a rock for 2 days now.</review>
